## Edges (Causal Relations) (44 relation(s) collapsed from duplicate extractions)

**Edge 1: AP2 complex → has_input → GluR2 \[merged 3 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Physical association with GluR2 cytoplasmic tail at residues K844-Q853; interaction with K844-Q853 region of GluR2 cytoplasmic tail; interaction with C-terminal tail of GluR2
- Assay: GST pull-down
- Figure: Fig 1A
- Reference: [PMID:12441055](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/12441055/) ✓ "Clathrin adaptor AP2 and NSF interact with overlapping sites of GluR2 and play distinct roles in AMPA receptor trafficking and hippocampal LTD." | DOI: [10.1016/s0896-6273(02)01024-3](https://doi.org/10.1016/s0896-6273(02)01024-3)
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "AP2 associates with a region of GluR2 that closely overlaps with the NSF binding site... amino acids K844-Q853... are necessary and sufficient for association with AP2."
- Quote: "amino acids K844-Q853 (“pep2r”) in the GluR2 tail are necessary and sufficient for association with AP2."
- Quote: "Pep2r, pep2m, and pep-A849-Q853 (200 uM) inhibited AP2 pull-down by GST-GluR2CT."

**Edge 2: NSF → has_input → GluR2 \[merged 3 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Physical association with GluR2 cytoplasmic tail; interaction with K844-Q853 region; stabilization of surface expression
- Assay: Coimmunoprecipitation
- Figure: Fig 1C
- Reference: [PMID:12441055](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/12441055/) ✓ "Clathrin adaptor AP2 and NSF interact with overlapping sites of GluR2 and play distinct roles in AMPA receptor trafficking and hippocampal LTD." | DOI: [10.1016/s0896-6273(02)01024-3](https://doi.org/10.1016/s0896-6273(02)01024-3)
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "a membrane-proximal region of the GluR2 cytoplasmic tail interacts with NSF"
- Quote: "Since the K844-Q853 region was also identified as the minimal NSF binding domain of GluR2"
- Quote: "NSF maintains synaptic strength by promoting the delivery/recycling of GluR2-containing AMPA receptors to the postsynaptic membrane."

**Edge 3: AP2 complex → directly_positively_regulates → GluR2 \[merged 2 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Endocytosis (internalization); endocytosis of GluR2 upon NMDA stimulation

- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "AP2 is involved specifically in NMDA receptor-induced (but not ligand-dependent) internalization of AMPA receptors"
- Quote: "mutants K844A and R845A (both defective in AP2 pull-down) failed to show increased internalization with NMDA"

**Edge 4: NSF → constitutively_upstream_of → GluR2 \[merged 2 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Stabilization/Maintenance of surface levels; stabilization of surface GluR2

- Confidence: MEDIUM
- Quote: "NSF function... is needed to maintain synaptic AMPA receptor responses, but is not directly required for NMDA receptor-mediated internalization"
- Quote: "blocking the NSF interaction leads to EPSC run-down but does not abolish subsequent LTD."

- Quote: "all membranes were probed with anti-β-adaptin antibody (1:1000, BD Biosciences), and anti-GluA1 or anti-HA (1:1000) antibody to control for amount precipitated."

**Edge 224: protein kinase A (PKA) → directly_positively_regulates → GluA1**
- Mechanism: phosphorylation of the Glu receptor 1 subunit
- Reference: [PMID:34369573](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/34369573/) ✓ "Phosphorylation of the AMPA receptor subunit GluA1 regulates clathrin-mediated receptor internalization." | DOI: [10.1242/jcs.257972](https://doi.org/10.1242/jcs.257972)

- Quote: "Regulation of {alpha}-amino-3-hydroxy-5-methyl-4-isoxazolepropionic acid receptor trafficking through PKA phosphorylation of the Glu receptor 1 subunit."

**Edge 225: calcineurin → directly_negatively_regulates → AMPA receptor**
- Mechanism: limiting synaptic incorporation
- Reference: [PMID:34369573](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/34369573/) ✓ "Phosphorylation of the AMPA receptor subunit GluA1 regulates clathrin-mediated receptor internalization." | DOI: [10.1242/jcs.257972](https://doi.org/10.1242/jcs.257972)

- Quote: "AKAP150-anchored calcineurin regulates synaptic plasticity by limiting synaptic incorporation of Ca2+-permeable AMPA receptors."

**Edge 226: PICK1 → has_input → GluR2 \[merged 6 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Calcium-dependent interaction, maximal at 15 µM Ca2+; Calcium-sensitive physical interaction; Physical interaction mediated by PICK1 Ca2+ sensing; binding interaction required for trafficking; Direct physical interaction (binding) that is regulated by Ca2+ concentration; Ca2+-dependent interaction
- Assay: co-immunoprecipitation (ECO:0000070) ✓
- Figure: Figure 1A
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "PICK1–GluR2 interactions are enhanced by the presence of 15 lM Ca2+."
- Quote: "These data demonstrate that the PICK1–GluR2 interaction in neurons is sensitive to Ca2+, and that PICK1 and GluR2 C-terminus mediate the Ca2+-sensitivity in this interaction."
- Quote: "The GST pull-down assays show that at all [Ca2+] tested, DNT PICK1 binds GluR2 as strongly as WT PICK1 in the presence of 15 mM Ca2+ (Figure 2B). Therefore, DNT PICK1 should bind strongly to GluR2 and stimulate its endocytosis"
- Quote: "PICK1 binds GluR2 but not GluR1 (Xia et al, 1999)"
- Quote: "The biphasic Ca2 þ-sensitivity of the PICK1–GluR2 interaction suggests that Ca2 þ may bind to multiple distinct sites on PICK1."
- Quote: "Activation of NMDARs ... results in a Ca2+ flux ... and therefore enhances binding of PICK1 to GluR2. (C) This results in increased AMPAR internalisation"

**Edge 227: Ca2+ → directly_positively_regulates → PICK1**
- Mechanism: Calcium binding induces conformational or affinity change in PICK1
- Assay: co-immunoprecipitation (ECO:0000070) ✓
- Figure: Figure 1A
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "We show that PICK1 is a Ca2+-binding protein, and that PICK1–GluR2 interactions are enhanced by the presence of 15 lM Ca2+."

**Edge 228: PICK1 → directly_positively_regulates → GluR2 \[merged 6 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Facilitating endocytosis through binding; Calcium-dependent modulation of interaction affinity; Calcium-dependent stimulation of GluR2 endocytosis; internalization / endocytosis; Stimulation of AMPAR endocytosis; enhanced interaction leads to AMPA receptor internalisation
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "PICK1 binds the AMPAR GluR2 subunit and is involved in AMPAR internalisation"
- Quote: "DNT PICK1 binds strongly to GST-R2C at all [Ca2+]free tested. Since both WT and DNT PICK1 are shown on the same Western blot, absolute levels of binding for this experiment can be directly compared."
- Quote: "When WT PICK1flag is expressed with mycGluR2, we observe a [Ca2+]O-dependent increase in internalised mycGluR2... Cells expressing mycGluR2 in the absence of PICK1flag showed basal levels of mycGluR2 internalisation"
- Quote: "Overexpression of WT PICK1 significantly enhances the NMDA-induced reduction of surface GluR2"
- Quote: "This suggests that PICK1 actively stimulates GluR2 internalisation."

- Mechanism: NMDAR activation induces AMPAR internalization
- Assay: surface biotinylation

**Edge 230: NMDAR → directly_positively_regulates → PICK1 \[merged 2 extractions\]**
- Mechanism: Calcium influx activates PICK1, enabling its interaction with GluR2; NMDAR-mediated Ca2+ influx increases local [Ca2+], which enhances PICK1 interaction with GluR2
- Assay: immunoprecipitation (ECO:0000085) ✓
- Figure: Figure 5A
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "PICK1 only stimulates AMPAR internalisation when NMDARs are activated, consistent with the requirement for a Ca2+ signal for optimal PICK1–GluR2 binding."
- Quote: "Activation of NMDARs localised in close proximity to AMPARs results in a Ca2+ flux that raises the local [Ca2+] to around 15 mM and therefore enhances binding of PICK1 to GluR2."

**Edge 231: NMDAR → indirectly_positively_regulates → PICK1**
- Mechanism: NMDAR-mediated Ca2+ influx is required for PICK1-mediated GluR2 endocytosis
- Assay: NMDAR activation with NMDA
- Figure: Figure 6
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"
- Confidence: HIGH
- Quote: "This is consistent with the requirement for a Ca2 þ signal (via NMDARs) for WT PICK1 to exert an effect on GluR2-containing AMPARs."

**Edge 232: PICK1 → indirectly_positively_regulates → protein kinase Calpha**
- Mechanism: targeting/recruitment to AMPA receptor clusters
- Reference: [PMID:7600801](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/7600801/) ✓ "Safe sex?"

**Edge 233: protein kinase Calpha → indirectly_negatively_regulates → AMPA receptor subunit 2**
